ADD _FillValue ATTRIBUTES?
The datasets/variables in the table below have integer source data, but no
_FillValue or missing_value attribute. We recommend adding the suggested
attributes to the variable's <addAttributes> in datasets.xml to identify
the default _FillValue used by ERDDAP. You can do this by hand or with the
addFillValueAttributes option in GenerateDatasetsXml.
If you don't make these changes, ERDDAP will treat those values (e.g., 127
for byte variables), if any, as valid data values (for example, on graphs
and when calculating statistics).
Or, if you decide a variable should not have a _FillValue attribute, you can add
  <att name="_FillValue">null</att>
instead, which will suppress this message for that datasetID+variable
combination in the future.
The list below is created each time you start up ERDDAP.
